_**Agent (claude-sonnet-4-20250514)**_

Found the issue! The problem is in the `workflow_agents` table. Looking at the migration and model files, I can see that:

1. The `workflow_agents` table does NOT have a `user_id` column - it has `created_by` instead (line 47 in migration)
2. But the API code in `/backend/app/api/workflows.py` and other files is trying to query `WorkflowAgent.query.filter_by(user_id=user.user_id)` which doesn't exist

The table has `created_by` field but the code is looking for `user_id`. Let me fix this:

_**Agent (claude-sonnet-4-20250514)**_

**Agent task list:**
- [‚ö°] üî• Fix WorkflowAgent queries to use created_by instead of user_id
- [ ] üî• Update all API endpoints that query workflow_agents table

   101‚Üí        if 'nodes' in data:

   113‚Üí            from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import insert
   114‚Üí            
   115‚Üí            for node_data in data['nodes']:
   116‚Üí                # Prepare node data for upsert

   118‚Üí                    'id': node_data['id'],
   119‚Üí                    'workflow_id': workflow.id,
   120‚Üí                    'node_type': node_data.get('type', 'unknown'),
   121‚Üí                    'position_x': node_data.get('position', {}).get('x', 0),
   122‚Üí                    'position_y': node_data.get('position', {}).get('y', 0),
   123‚Üí                    'data': node_data.get('data', {}),
   124‚Üí                    'configured': node_data.get('data', {}).get('configured', False),
   125‚Üí                    'updated_at': datetime.utcnow()
   126‚Üí                }
   127‚Üí                
   128‚Üí                # Use PostgreSQL UPSERT (INSERT ... ON CONFLICT ... DO UPDATE)
   129‚Üí                stmt = insert(WorkflowNode).values(**node_values)
   130‚Üí                stmt = stmt.on_conflict_do_update(
   131‚Üí                    index_elements=['id'],
   132‚Üí                    set_=dict(
   133‚Üí                        workflow_id=stmt.excluded.workflow_id,
   134‚Üí                        node_type=stmt.excluded.node_type,
   135‚Üí                        position_x=stmt.excluded.position_x,
   136‚Üí                        position_y=stmt.excluded.position_y,
   137‚Üí                        data=stmt.excluded.data,
   138‚Üí                        configured=stmt.excluded.configured,
   139‚Üí                        updated_at=stmt.excluded.updated_at
   140‚Üí                    )
   141‚Üí                )
   142‚Üí                db.session.execute(stmt)
   143‚Üí        
   144‚Üí        if 'edges' in data:
   145‚Üí            workflow.edges = data['edges']
   146‚Üí        
   147‚Üí        if 'name' in data:
   148‚Üí            workflow.name = data['name']
   149‚Üí        
   150‚Üí        db.session.commit()
   151‚Üí        
   152‚Üí        return jsonify({
   153‚Üí            'success': True,
   154‚Üí            'workflow': workflow.to_dict()
   155‚Üí        })
   156‚Üí        
   157‚Üí    except Exception as e:
   158‚Üí        db.session.rollback()

   236‚Üí        if not user:
   237‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'User not authenticated'}), 401
   238‚Üí

   240‚Üí        agent = WorkflowAgent.query.filter_by(user_id=user.user_id).first()

   243‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Agent not found'}), 404

   246‚Üí        workflow = AgentWorkflow.query.filter_by(
   247‚Üí            agent_id=agent_id,
   248‚Üí            user_id=user.user_id
   249‚Üí        ).first()

   252‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Workflow not found'}), 404
   253‚Üí

   255‚Üí        node = WorkflowNode.query.filter_by(
   256‚Üí            id=node_id,
   257‚Üí            workflow_id=workflow.id
   258‚Üí        ).first()
   259‚Üí        
   260‚Üí        if node:
   261‚Üí            db.session.delete(node)
   262‚Üí        
   263‚Üí        # Remove from workflow nodes array
   264‚Üí        workflow_nodes = workflow.nodes or []
   265‚Üí        workflow.nodes = [n for n in workflow_nodes if n.get('id') != node_id]
   266‚Üí        
   267‚Üí        # Remove from workflow edges array
   268‚Üí        workflow_edges = workflow.edges or []
   269‚Üí        workflow.edges = [
   270‚Üí            e for e in workflow_edges 
   271‚Üí            if e.get('source') != node_id and e.get('target') != node_id
   272‚Üí        ]
   273‚Üí        
   274‚Üí        db.session.commit()
   275‚Üí        
   276‚Üí        return jsonify({'success': True})
   277‚Üí        
   278‚Üí    except Exception as e:
   279‚Üí        db.session.rollback()
   280‚Üí        logger.error(f"Error deleting workflow node: {e}")
   281‚Üí        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': str(e)}), 500

1‚Üífrom flask import request, jsonify
     2‚Üífrom app.api import api_bp
     3‚Üífrom app.models.execution import WorkflowExecution, NodeExecution
     4‚Üífrom app.models.agent import WorkflowAgent
     5‚Üífrom app.auth import auth_required, get_current_user
     6‚Üífrom app import db
     7‚Üífrom datetime import datetime
     8‚Üíimport logging
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üílogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    11‚Üí
    12‚Üí
    13‚Üí@api_bp.route('/agents/<int:agent_id>/executions', methods=['GET'])
    14‚Üí@auth_required
    15‚Üídef get_agent_executions(agent_id):
    16‚Üí    """Get execution history for a specific agent"""
    17‚Üí    try:
    18‚Üí        user = get_current_user()
    19‚Üí        if not user:
    20‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'User not authenticated'}), 401
    21‚Üí        
    22‚Üí        # Verify agent ownership
    23‚Üí        agent = WorkflowAgent.query.filter_by(user_id=user.user_id).first()
    24‚Üí        
    25‚Üí        if not agent:
    26‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Agent not found'}), 404
    27‚Üí        
    28‚Üí        # Get executions ordered by most recent first
    29‚Üí        executions = WorkflowExecution.query.filter_by(
    30‚Üí            agent_id=agent_id,
    31‚Üí            user_id=user.user_id
    32‚Üí        ).order_by(WorkflowExecution.started_at.desc()).limit(20).all()
    33‚Üí        
    34‚Üí        return jsonify({
    35‚Üí            'success': True,
    36‚Üí            'executions': [execution.to_dict() for execution in executions]
    37‚Üí        })
    38‚Üí

    86‚Üídef create_node_execution(execution_id):
    87‚Üí    """Create a node execution record"""
    88‚Üí    try:
    89‚Üí        user = get_current_user()
    90‚Üí        if not user:
    91‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'User not authenticated'}), 401
    92‚Üí

    96‚Üí            user_id=user.user_id
    97‚Üí        ).first()
    98‚Üí        
    99‚Üí        if not execution:
   100‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Execution not found'}), 404
   101‚Üí

   106‚Üí            execution_id=execution_id,
   107‚Üí            node_id=data['node_id'],
   108‚Üí            node_type=data['node_type'],
   109‚Üí            input_config=data.get('input_config'),
   110‚Üí            status='running'
   111‚Üí        )
   112‚Üí

   118‚Üí                'selectors': data.get('selectors'),
   119‚Üí                'loop_config': data.get('loopConfig')

   123‚Üí                'ai_prompt': data.get('ai_prompt'),
   124‚Üí                'ai_model': data.get('ai_model', 'gpt-4o-mini')
   125‚Üí            }

   127‚Üí            node_specific_data = {
   128‚Üí                'model_type': data.get('model_type', 'linear_regression'),

   130‚Üí                'user_instructions': data.get('user_instructions'),
   131‚Üí                'training_config': data.get('training_config')
   132‚Üí            }
   133‚Üí        elif data['node_type'] == 'httpRequest':
   134‚Üí            node_specific_data = {
   135‚Üí                'method': data.get('method', 'GET'),
   136‚Üí                'url': data.get('url'),
   137‚Üí                'auth_type': data.get('auth_type')
   138‚Üí            }
   139‚Üí        
   140‚Üí        # Remove None values to keep JSONB clean
   141‚Üí        node_specific_data = {k: v for k, v in node_specific_data.items() if v is not None}
   142‚Üí        node_execution.node_specific_data = node_specific_data if node_specific_data else None
   143‚Üí

   158‚Üí@api_bp.route('/executions/nodes/<int:node_execution_id>', methods=['PUT'])
   159‚Üí@auth_required
   160‚Üídef update_node_execution(node_execution_id):
   161‚Üí    """Update a node execution with results"""
   162‚Üí    try:
   163‚Üí        user = get_current_user()
   164‚Üí        if not user:
   165‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'User not authenticated'}), 401
   166‚Üí        
   167‚Üí        # Verify ownership through execution
   168‚Üí        node_execution = NodeExecution.query.join(WorkflowExecution).filter(
   169‚Üí            NodeExecution.id == node_execution_id,
   170‚Üí            WorkflowExecution.user_id == user.user_id
   171‚Üí        ).first()
   172‚Üí        
   173‚Üí        if not node_execution:
   174‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Node execution not found'}), 404
   175‚Üí        
   176‚Üí        data = request.get_json()
   177‚Üí        
   178‚Üí        # Update execution results
   179‚Üí        node_execution.completed_at = datetime.utcnow()
   180‚Üí        node_execution.status = data.get('status', 'completed')
   181‚Üí        node_execution.error_message = data.get('error_message')
   182‚Üí        node_execution.output_data = data.get('output_data')
   183‚Üí        
   184‚Üí        # Update node-specific results in JSONB field
   185‚Üí        current_data = node_execution.node_specific_data or {}
   186‚Üí        
   187‚Üí        if node_execution.node_type == 'webSource':
   188‚Üí            current_data['extracted_data'] = data.get('extracted_data')
   189‚Üí        elif node_execution.node_type == 'aiProcessor':
   190‚Üí            current_data['ai_output'] = data.get('ai_output')
   191‚Üí            current_data['ai_tokens_used'] = data.get('ai_tokens_used')
   192‚Üí        elif node_execution.node_type == 'linearRegression':
   193‚Üí            # Parse ML results from output_data if it contains model training results
   194‚Üí            output_data = data.get('output_data', {})
   195‚Üí            if isinstance(output_data, dict):
   196‚Üí                current_data['model_metrics'] = output_data.get('metrics')
   197‚Üí                current_data['model_features'] = output_data.get('features')
   198‚Üí                current_data['model_coefficients'] = output_data.get('coefficients')
   199‚Üí                current_data['preprocessing_notes'] = output_data.get('preprocessing_notes')
   200‚Üí            current_data['ai_tokens_used'] = data.get('ai_tokens_used')
   201‚Üí        elif node_execution.node_type == 'httpRequest':
   202‚Üí            # Update HTTP-specific results
   203‚Üí            current_data['status_code'] = data.get('status_code')
   204‚Üí            current_data['response_time'] = data.get('response_time')
   205‚Üí            current_data['response_size'] = data.get('response_size')
   206‚Üí            current_data['response_headers'] = data.get('response_headers')
   207‚Üí        
   208‚Üí        # Remove None values and update
   209‚Üí        current_data = {k: v for k, v in current_data.items() if v is not None}
   210‚Üí        node_execution.node_specific_data = current_data if current_data else None
   211‚Üí        
   212‚Üí        db.session.commit()
   213‚Üí        
   214‚Üí        return jsonify({
   215‚Üí            'success': True,
   216‚Üí            'node_execution': node_execution.to_dict()
   217‚Üí        })
   218‚Üí        
   219‚Üí    except Exception as e:
   220‚Üí        logger.error(f"Error updating node execution: {e}")
   221‚Üí        db.session.rollback()
   222‚Üí        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': str(e)}), 500
   223‚Üí

   291‚Üí@api_bp.route('/agents/<int:agent_id>/nodes/<node_id>/executions', methods=['GET'])
   292‚Üí@auth_required
   293‚Üídef get_node_execution_history(agent_id, node_id):
   294‚Üí    """Get execution history for a specific node"""
   295‚Üí    try:
   296‚Üí        user = get_current_user()
   297‚Üí        if not user:
   298‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'User not authenticated'}), 401
   299‚Üí        
   300‚Üí        # Verify agent ownership
   301‚Üí        agent = WorkflowAgent.query.filter_by(user_id=user.user_id).first()
   302‚Üí        
   303‚Üí        if not agent:
   304‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Agent not found'}), 404
   305‚Üí        
   306‚Üí        # Get node executions ordered by most recent first
   307‚Üí        node_executions = NodeExecution.query.join(WorkflowExecution).filter(
   308‚Üí            NodeExecution.node_id == node_id,
   309‚Üí            WorkflowExecution.agent_id == agent_id,
   310‚Üí            WorkflowExecution.user_id == user.user_id
   311‚Üí        ).order_by(NodeExecution.started_at.desc()).limit(50).all()
   312‚Üí        
   313‚Üí        logger.info(f"üîç Found {len(node_executions)} executions for node {node_id}")
   314‚Üí        
   315‚Üí        # Debug: Log all node executions for this agent to see what we have
   316‚Üí        all_node_executions = NodeExecution.query.join(WorkflowExecution).filter(
   317‚Üí            WorkflowExecution.agent_id == agent_id,
   318‚Üí            WorkflowExecution.user_id == user.user_id
   319‚Üí        ).all()
   320‚Üí        
   321‚Üí        logger.info(f"üîç All node executions for agent {agent_id}:")
   322‚Üí        for exec in all_node_executions:
   323‚Üí            logger.info(f"  - Node ID: {exec.node_id}, Type: {exec.node_type}, Status: {exec.status}")
   324‚Üí        
   325‚Üí        return jsonify({
   326‚Üí            'success': True,
   327‚Üí            'executions': [execution.to_dict() for execution in node_executions]
   328‚Üí        })
   329‚Üí        
   330‚Üí    except Exception as e:
   331‚Üí        logger.error(f"Error getting node execution history: {e}")
   332‚Üí        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': str(e)}), 500

   149‚Üí                return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Selectors must be a list'}), 400
   150‚Üí            job.selectors = data['selectors']
   151‚Üí        if 'frequency' in data:
   152‚Üí            job.frequency = data['frequency']
   153‚Üí        if 'change_threshold' in data:
   154‚Üí            job.change_threshold = data['change_threshold']
   155‚Üí        if 'is_active' in data:

   266‚Üí@api_bp.route('/css-selector/generate', methods=['POST'])
   267‚Üí@auth_required
   268‚Üídef generate_css_selector():
   269‚Üí    """Generate CSS selectors for elements on a webpage"""
   270‚Üí    try:
   271‚Üí        data = request.get_json()
   272‚Üí        
   273‚Üí        if 'url' not in data:
   274‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'URL is required'}), 400
   275‚Üí        
   276‚Üí        url = data['url']
   277‚Üí        element_text = data.get('element_text', '')
   278‚Üí        element_attributes = data.get('element_attributes', {})
   279‚Üí        
   280‚Üí        # Validate URL
   281‚Üí        if not url.startswith(('http://', 'https://')):
   282‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Invalid URL format'}), 400
   283‚Üí        
   284‚Üí        # Generate selectors using Playwright
   285‚Üí        loop = asyncio.new_event_loop()
   286‚Üí        asyncio.set_event_loop(loop)
   287‚Üí        
   288‚Üí        try:
   289‚Üí            async def generate_selectors():
   290‚Üí                async with PlaywrightService() as service:
   291‚Üí                    await service.load_page(url, wait_for_load=True)
   292‚Üí                    
   293‚Üí                    selectors = await service.generate_css_selector(
   294‚Üí                        element_text, element_attributes
   295‚Üí                    )
   296‚Üí                    
   297‚Üí                    # Test each selector
   298‚Üí                    tested_selectors = []
   299‚Üí                    for selector in selectors[:5]:  # Limit to 5 selectors
   300‚Üí                        test_result = await service.test_selector(selector)
   301‚Üí                        tested_selectors.append(test_result)
   302‚Üí                    
   303‚Üí                    page_info = await service.get_page_info()
   304‚Üí                    
   305‚Üí                    return {
   306‚Üí                        'selectors': tested_selectors,
   307‚Üí                        'page_info': page_info,
   308‚Üí                        'search_criteria': {
   309‚Üí                            'text': element_text,
   310‚Üí                            'attributes': element_attributes
   311‚Üí                        }
   312‚Üí                    }
   313‚Üí            
   314‚Üí            result = loop.run_until_complete(generate_selectors())
   315‚Üí            
   316‚Üí            return jsonify({
   317‚Üí                'success': True,
   318‚Üí                'result': result
   319‚Üí            })
   320‚Üí            
   321‚Üí        finally:
   322‚Üí            loop.close()
   323‚Üí        
   324‚Üí    except Exception as e:
   325‚Üí        logger.error(f"Error generating CSS selector: {e}")
   326‚Üí        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': str(e)}), 500
   327‚Üí
   328‚Üí

   379‚Üí@api_bp.route('/css-selector/extract', methods=['POST'])
   380‚Üí@auth_required
   381‚Üídef extract_data_preview():
   382‚Üí    """Extract data from multiple elements using CSS selectors"""
   383‚Üí    try:
   384‚Üí        data = request.get_json()
   385‚Üí        
   386‚Üí        if 'url' not in data:
   387‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'URL is required'}), 400
   388‚Üí        
   389‚Üí        if 'selectors' not in data or not isinstance(data['selectors'], list):
   390‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Selectors list is required'}), 400
   391‚Üí        
   392‚Üí        url = data['url']
   393‚Üí        selectors = data['selectors']
   394‚Üí        
   395‚Üí        # Validate URL
   396‚Üí        if not url.startswith(('http://', 'https://')):
   397‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Invalid URL format'}), 400
   398‚Üí        
   399‚Üí        # Extract data using Playwright
   400‚Üí        loop = asyncio.new_event_loop()
   401‚Üí        asyncio.set_event_loop(loop)
   402‚Üí        
   403‚Üí        try:
   404‚Üí            async def extract_data():
   405‚Üí                async with PlaywrightService() as service:
   406‚Üí                    await service.load_page(url, wait_for_load=True)
   407‚Üí                    
   408‚Üí                    # Extract data from all matching elements
   409‚Üí                    extracted_data = await service.extract_all_content(selectors)
   410‚Üí                    
   411‚Üí                    # Also get page info
   412‚Üí                    page_info = await service.get_page_info()
   413‚Üí                    
   414‚Üí                    return {
   415‚Üí                        'extracted_data': extracted_data,
   416‚Üí                        'page_info': page_info,
   417‚Üí                        'row_count': len(extracted_data),
   418‚Üí                        'selectors_used': len(selectors)
   419‚Üí                    }
   420‚Üí            
   421‚Üí            result = loop.run_until_complete(extract_data())
   422‚Üí            
   423‚Üí            return jsonify({
   424‚Üí                'success': True,
   425‚Üí                'result': result
   426‚Üí            })
   427‚Üí            
   428‚Üí        finally:
   429‚Üí            loop.close()
   430‚Üí        
   431‚Üí    except Exception as e:
   432‚Üí        logger.error(f"Error extracting data: {e}")
   433‚Üí        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': str(e)}), 500
   434‚Üí

   436‚Üí@api_bp.route('/monitoring-jobs/<int:job_id>/changes', methods=['GET'])
   437‚Üí@auth_required
   438‚Üídef get_job_changes(job_id):
   439‚Üí    """Get change history for a monitoring job"""
   440‚Üí    try:
   441‚Üí        user = get_current_user()
   442‚Üí        if not user:
   443‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'User not authenticated'}), 401
   444‚Üí        
   445‚Üí        # Verify job ownership
   446‚Üí        job = MonitoringJob.query.filter_by(
   447‚Üí            id=job_id,
   448‚Üí            user_id=user.user_id
   449‚Üí        ).first()
   450‚Üí        
   451‚Üí        if not job:
   452‚Üí            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Monitoring job not found'}), 404
   453‚Üí        
   454‚Üí        # Get changes with pagination
   455‚Üí        page = request.args.get('page', 1, type=int)
   456‚Üí        per_page = min(request.args.get('per_page', 20, type=int), 100)
   457‚Üí        
   458‚Üí        changes = ChangeRecord.query.filter_by(
   459‚Üí            monitoring_job_id=job_id
   460‚Üí        ).order_by(ChangeRecord.detected_at.desc()).paginate(
   461‚Üí            page=page, per_page=per_page, error_out=False
   462‚Üí        )
   463‚Üí        
   464‚Üí        return jsonify({
   465‚Üí            'success': True,
   466‚Üí            'changes': [change.to_dict() for change in changes.items],
   467‚Üí            'pagination': {
   468‚Üí                'page': changes.page,
   469‚Üí                'pages': changes.pages,
   470‚Üí                'per_page': changes.per_page,
   471‚Üí                'total': changes.total
   472‚Üí            }
   473‚Üí        })
   474‚Üí        
   475‚Üí    except Exception as e:
   476‚Üí        logger.error(f"Error getting job changes: {e}")
   477‚Üí        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': str(e)}), 500

Perfect! Now that the `PLAYWRIGHT_BROWSERS_PATH` is commented out in your `.env` file, you just need to:

- `.env.example` with better documentation
- `CLAUDE.md` to warn users not to set this variable unless using Docker

This fix will work for all users - they just need to leave `PLAYWRIGHT_BROWSERS_PATH` unset (commented out) in their `.env` file.

   150‚Üí        """Generate a robust CSS selector for a specific element"""

    81‚Üí// Prediction Interface Component
    82‚Üíinterface PredictionInterfaceProps {
    83‚Üí  features: string[];
    84‚Üí  targetName: string;
    85‚Üí  modelId: number;
    86‚Üí  authHeaders: Record<string, string>;
    87‚Üí}
    88‚Üí
    89‚Üíconst PredictionInterface: React.FC<PredictionInterfaceProps> = ({ 
    90‚Üí  features, 
    91‚Üí  targetName, 
    92‚Üí  modelId, 
    93‚Üí  authHeaders 
    94‚Üí}) => {
    95‚Üí  const [featureValues, setFeatureValues] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});
    96‚Üí  const [prediction, setPrediction] = useState<number | null>(null);
    97‚Üí  const [predicting, setPredicting] = useState(false);
    98‚Üí  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
    99‚Üí
   100‚Üí  const handleFeatureChange = (feature: string, value: string) => {
   101‚Üí    setFeatureValues(prev => ({ ...prev, [feature]: value }));
   102‚Üí    // Clear previous prediction when inputs change
   103‚Üí    setPrediction(null);
   104‚Üí    setError(null);
   105‚Üí  };
   106‚Üí
   107‚Üí  const handlePredict = async () => {
   108‚Üí    // Validate all features have values
   109‚Üí    const missingFeatures = features.filter(feature => !featureValues[feature]?.trim());
   110‚Üí    if (missingFeatures.length > 0) {
   111‚Üí      setError(`Please provide values for: ${missingFeatures.join(', ')}`);
   112‚Üí      return;
   113‚Üí    }
   114‚Üí
   115‚Üí    setPredicting(true);
   116‚Üí    setError(null);
   117‚Üí
   118‚Üí    try {
   119‚Üí      // Convert string values to numbers
   120‚Üí      const numericFeatures: Record<string, number> = {};
   121‚Üí      for (const feature of features) {
   122‚Üí        const value = featureValues[feature];
   123‚Üí        const numValue = parseFloat(value);
   124‚Üí        if (isNaN(numValue)) {
   125‚Üí          throw new Error(`Invalid number for ${feature}: ${value}`);
   126‚Üí        }
   127‚Üí        numericFeatures[feature] = numValue;
   128‚Üí      }
   129‚Üí
   130‚Üí      const response = await fetch(`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASE_URL}/api/v1/ml/models/${modelId}/predict`, {
   131‚Üí        method: 'POST',
   132‚Üí        headers: {
   133‚Üí          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   134‚Üí          ...authHeaders
   135‚Üí        },
   136‚Üí        body: JSON.stringify({
   137‚Üí          input_data: [numericFeatures]
   138‚Üí        })
   139‚Üí      });
   140‚Üí
   141‚Üí      if (!response.ok) {
   142‚Üí        const errorData = await response.json();
   143‚Üí        throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Prediction failed');
   144‚Üí      }
   145‚Üí
   146‚Üí      const result = await response.json();
   147‚Üí      if (result.success && result.predictions && result.predictions.length > 0) {
   148‚Üí        setPrediction(result.predictions[0]);
   149‚Üí      } else {
   150‚Üí        throw new Error('No prediction returned');
   151‚Üí      }
   152‚Üí    } catch (err) {
   153‚Üí      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Prediction failed');
   154‚Üí    } finally {
   155‚Üí      setPredicting(false);
   156‚Üí    }
   157‚Üí  };
   158‚Üí
   159‚Üí  return (
   160‚Üí    <div className="border-t border-border-subtle/50 pt-3 mt-3">
   161‚Üí      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
   162‚Üí        <Calculator className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
   163‚Üí        <span className="font-medium text-text-primary text-sm">Make Prediction</span>
   164‚Üí      </div>
   165‚Üí      
   166‚Üí      <div className="space-y-2">
   167‚Üí        {features.map((feature) => (
   168‚Üí          <div key={feature} className="flex items-center gap-2">
   169‚Üí            <label className="text-xs text-text-muted min-w-[80px] truncate" title={feature}>
   170‚Üí              {feature}:
   171‚Üí            </label>
   172‚Üí            <input
   173‚Üí              type="number"
   174‚Üí              step="any"
   175‚Üí              value={featureValues[feature] || ''}
   176‚Üí              onChange={(e) => handleFeatureChange(feature, e.target.value)}
   177‚Üí              className="flex-1 text-xs bg-background border border-border-subtle rounded px-2 py-1 focus:border-primary focus:outline-none"
   178‚Üí              placeholder="Enter value..."
   179‚Üí            />
   180‚Üí          </div>
   181‚Üí        ))}
   182‚Üí      </div>
   183‚Üí
   184‚Üí      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-3">
   185‚Üí        <button
   186‚Üí          onClick={handlePredict}
   187‚Üí          disabled={predicting || features.some(f => !featureValues[f]?.trim())}
   188‚Üí          className="flex items-center gap-1 px-3 py-1.5 bg-primary hover:bg-primary-hover disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed text-white text-xs rounded transition-colors"
   189‚Üí        >
   190‚Üí          {predicting ? (
   191‚Üí            <>
   192‚Üí              <Loader2 className="w-3 h-3 animate-spin" />
   193‚Üí              Predicting...
   194‚Üí            </>
   195‚Üí          ) : (
   196‚Üí            <>
   197‚Üí              <Target className="w-3 h-3" />
   198‚Üí              Predict {targetName}
   199‚Üí            </>
   200‚Üí          )}

_**Agent (claude-opus-4-20250514)**_

<think><details>This is a great architectural question about adding a dashboard feature to the workflow engine. The user wants to create a professional dashboard system where:

1. Users can arrange widgets (graphs, model interfaces, text boxes, etc.)
2. Widgets can be connected to workflow outputs
3. The dashboard should be both:
   - Available as a tab for self-hosted users
   - Publishable/hostable separately while still connected to workflows

This is a complex feature that requires careful planning. Let me think about the architecture:

Key considerations:
1. **Separation of concerns**: Dashboards and workflows should be separate entities but connectable
2. **Publishing mechanism**: Need a way to publish dashboards publicly while keeping workflows private
3. **Real-time updates**: Dashboard widgets need to update when workflow data changes
4. **Security**: Published dashboards shouldn't expose sensitive workflow details
5. **Flexibility**: Users should be able to create both private and public dashboards

Possible architecture:
1. Create a new `Dashboard` entity that can reference workflow outputs
2. Dashboard widgets can subscribe to specific node outputs via a publish/subscribe pattern
3. For public dashboards, create a separate "Dashboard Viewer" mode that only shows the dashboard without workflow access
4. Use websockets or polling for real-time updates
5. Dashboard configuration stored separately from workflow configuration

I should use the TodoWrite tool to plan this feature properly.</details></think>

_**Agent (claude-opus-4-20250514)**_

## Dashboard Architecture Proposal

You're absolutely right about the complexity here. Here's my recommendation for a flexible, scalable architecture:

### 1. **Dual-Mode Dashboard System**

Create dashboards that can operate in two modes:
- **Integrated Mode**: Dashboard as a tab within the workflow builder (for self-hosted users)
- **Standalone Mode**: Published dashboards accessible via unique URLs without workflow access

### 2. **Core Architecture Components**

```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ                   WORKFLOW ENGINE                        ‚îÇ
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
‚îÇ  Workflows  ‚îÇ  Dashboards  ‚îÇ  Data Bindings  ‚îÇ  Widgets ‚îÇ
‚îÇ             ‚îÇ              ‚îÇ                  ‚îÇ          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  - Nodes    ‚îÇ  - Layout    ‚îÇ  - Node Output  ‚îÇ  - Chart ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  - Edges    ‚îÇ  - Widgets   ‚îÇ    Mappings     ‚îÇ  - Table ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  - Execute  ‚îÇ  - Config    ‚îÇ  - Refresh      ‚îÇ  - Model ‚îÇ
‚îÇ             ‚îÇ  - Public?   ‚îÇ    Rules        ‚îÇ  - Text  ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
                              ‚îÇ
                              ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Private Access (Full UI)
                              ‚îÇ
                              ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Public Access (Viewer Only)
```

### 3. **Data Model Design**

```typescript
// Dashboard entity
interface Dashboard {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  agentId: number; // Links to workflow agent
  userId: number;
  
  // Layout & widgets
  layout: GridLayout;
  widgets: Widget[];
  
  // Publishing
  isPublic: boolean;
  publicUrl?: string;
  publicKey?: string; // For secure access
  
  // Settings
  refreshInterval?: number;
  theme?: DashboardTheme;
  
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

// Widget entity
interface Widget {
  id: string;
  type: 'chart' | 'table' | 'metric' | 'model-interface' | 'text';
  
  // Position in grid
  gridPosition: GridPosition;
  
  // Data binding
  dataSource: {
    nodeId: string;
    outputPath?: string; // For nested data
    transform?: DataTransform;
  };
  
  // Widget-specific config
  config: WidgetConfig;
  
  // Display
  title?: string;
  description?: string;
}
```

### 4. **Implementation Strategy**

**Phase 1: Integrated Dashboards**
- Add "Dashboard" tab next to "Workflow" and "History"
- Grid-based layout system (like React Grid Layout)
- Basic widget types: Chart, Table, Metric Card, Text
- Direct binding to workflow node outputs
- Real-time updates when workflows run

**Phase 2: Publishing System**
- Generate unique public URLs for dashboards
- Public API endpoint that serves dashboard data without exposing workflows
- Caching layer for performance
- Optional authentication for semi-public dashboards

**Phase 3: Advanced Features**
- Interactive widgets (forms that trigger workflows)
- Custom widget types
- Dashboard templates
- Embedding dashboards in other sites

### 5. **Technical Implementation**

```typescript
// Example API structure
/api/v1/dashboards          // CRUD for dashboards
/api/v1/dashboards/:id/widgets  // Manage widgets
/api/v1/dashboards/:id/data     // Get latest data for all widgets
/api/v1/public/dashboards/:publicKey  // Public access
```

### 6. **Security Considerations**

- Workflows remain private, only dashboard data is exposed
- Public dashboards get read-only snapshots of data
- Rate limiting on public endpoints
- Optional password protection for published dashboards
- Data sanitization before public exposure

### My Recommendation:

Start with **integrated dashboards** (as a tab) first. This gives you:
1. Immediate value for self-hosted users
2. Time to refine the widget system
3. Real user feedback before building the publishing system

Once that's solid, add the publishing layer as a separate feature that:
- Creates a read-only view of the dashboard

- Provides a clean, embeddable viewer

```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê    API     ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê

            ‚îÇ                                       ‚îÇ
            ‚îÇ                                       ‚îÇ
        Docker Container                    Docker Container

## Implementation Strategy:

### 1. **Extend Workflow Engine API**
Add dashboard-specific endpoints to your existing backend:
```typescript
// Dashboard data endpoints
GET /api/v1/dashboards/:dashboardId/widgets/:widgetId/data
GET /api/v1/agents/:agentId/latest-execution
GET /api/v1/nodes/:nodeId/output
POST /api/v1/webhooks/dashboard-update  // For real-time updates
```

### 2. **Separate Dashboard Application**
Create a new React app in `/dashboard/` that:
- Connects to workflow engine via API
- Has its own Docker setup
- Can be deployed independently
- Uses environment variables to configure API endpoints

### 3. **Configuration via Environment**
```bash
# Dashboard .env
VITE_WORKFLOW_API_URL=http://localhost:5000
VITE_WORKFLOW_API_KEY=your-api-key
VITE_DASHBOARD_CONFIG=/config/dashboard.json
```

### 4. **Dashboard Configuration File**
```json
{
  "title": "My Analytics Dashboard",
  "theme": "dark",
  "refreshInterval": 5000,
  "widgets": [
    {
      "id": "chart-1",
      "type": "chart",
      "title": "Sales Trends",
      "position": { "x": 0, "y": 0, "w": 6, "h": 4 },
      "dataSource": {
        "agentId": 1,
        "nodeId": "chart-node-1",
        "refreshOnWorkflowComplete": true
      },
      "config": {
        "chartType": "line",
        "xAxis": "date",
        "yAxis": "sales"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

1. **Zero Vendor Lock-in**: Users own their dashboard deployment
2. **Flexible Integration**: Dashboard can be embedded in existing apps
3. **Scalable**: Multiple dashboards can connect to one workflow engine
4. **Simple**: No complex publishing system needed
5. **Customizable**: Users can modify dashboard code as needed

Let me think through the options:

1. **Same repo (monorepo)**:

   - Cons: Larger repo, harder to version independently

   - workflow-engine repo
   - workflow-dashboard repo  
   - Pros: Independent versioning, separate CI/CD, cleaner separation
   - Cons: Harder to keep APIs in sync, more complex development setup

   - Main repo with both
   - Separate repo for dashboard-only deployments

- The dashboard is tightly coupled to the workflow engine API
- Shared TypeScript types/interfaces
- Easier to maintain API compatibility
- Simpler for users to get started
- Can always split later if needed

_**Agent (claude-sonnet-4-20250514)**_

Great question! I'd recommend a **monorepo approach** initially, then potentially splitting later. Here's why:

## Option 1: Monorepo (Recommended)

```
workflow-engine/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ backend/                 # Existing workflow engine
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ frontend/               # Existing workflow builder UI  
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ dashboard/              # New standalone dashboard app
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ shared/                 # Shared types, utilities
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ docker-compose.yml      # Run both services together
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ docker-compose.prod.yml # Production setup
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ README.md               # Updated with dashboard info
```

**Benefits:**
- **Shared TypeScript types** between workflow engine and dashboard
- **API compatibility** - easier to keep them in sync
- **Simpler development** - one git clone, coordinated releases
- **Easier for users** - single repo to fork/deploy
- **Shared CI/CD** - test compatibility between services

## Implementation Structure:

### Backend API Extensions
```typescript
// shared/types/dashboard.ts
export interface DashboardWidget {
  id: string;
  type: 'chart' | 'table' | 'metric' | 'model-interface';
  dataSource: {
    agentId: number;
    nodeId: string;
    outputPath?: string;
  };
  config: Record<string, any>;
}

// Both backend and dashboard can import this
```

### Docker Setup
```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'
services:
  workflow-engine:
    build: ./backend
    ports:
      - "5000:5000"
    
  dashboard:
    build: ./dashboard
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    environment:
      - VITE_WORKFLOW_API_URL=http://workflow-engine:5000
    depends_on:
      - workflow-engine
```

### Package.json Scripts
```json
{
  "scripts": {
    "dev": "concurrently \"npm run dev:backend\" \"npm run dev:dashboard\"",
    "dev:backend": "cd backend && npm run dev",
    "dev:dashboard": "cd dashboard && npm run dev",
    "build": "npm run build:backend && npm run build:dashboard",
    "docker:up": "docker-compose up -d"
  }
}
```

## Option 2: Separate Repos (Future consideration)

If you later want to split them:
- `workflow-engine` - Core engine repo
- `workflow-dashboard` - Dashboard-only repo
- `workflow-types` - Shared types package (npm)

## My Recommendation:

**Start with monorepo** because:
1. You're in early development - easier to iterate
2. API will change frequently - easier to keep in sync
3. Users want simple setup - one clone, one docker-compose
4. Can always split later when mature

The workflow would be:
1. User clones the repo
2. Runs `docker-compose up` 
3. Gets both workflow engine (port 5000) and dashboard (port 3001)
4. Can deploy dashboard separately by just building the `/dashboard` folder

Want me to start setting up this structure? I'd begin by:
1. Creating the `/dashboard` folder structure
2. Setting up shared types in `/shared`
3. Adding dashboard-specific API endpoints to the backend
4. Creating the docker setup

What do you think?

# Dashboard System Implementation Plan

## Architecture Overview

I'm implementing a professional-grade dashboard system that connects to the workflow engine. Here's my comprehensive plan:

_**Agent (claude-sonnet-4-20250514)**_

Tool use: **Write**

```md
# Dashboard System Architecture

## Overview

The Dashboard System is a standalone React application that connects to the Workflow Engine to create customizable, real-time data visualization dashboards.

## Architecture Principles

### 1. Microservices Design
- **Workflow Engine**: Backend data processing service (Port 5000)
- **Dashboard App**: Frontend visualization service (Port 3001)
- **Shared Types**: Common TypeScript definitions
- **Independent Deployment**: Each service can be deployed separately

### 2. Technology Stack

**Dashboard Frontend:**
- React 18 + TypeScript
- Vite (build tool)
- Tailwind CSS (styling)
- React Grid Layout (drag-and-drop grid)
- Recharts (data visualization)
- Zustand (state management)
- React Query (data fetching)

**Testing Stack:**
- Vitest (unit testing)
- React Testing Library (component testing)
- Playwright (E2E testing)
- MSW (API mocking)

### 3. Data Flow

\```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê    HTTP/WS    ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ Workflow Engine ‚îÇ‚óÑ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚ñ∫‚îÇ Dashboard App   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                 ‚îÇ               ‚îÇ                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ - Execute nodes ‚îÇ               ‚îÇ - Render widgets‚îÇ
‚îÇ - Store results ‚îÇ               ‚îÇ - Update layouts‚îÇ
‚îÇ - Send updates  ‚îÇ               ‚îÇ - Handle config ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò               ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
\```

## Core Components

### 1. Widget System
- **Chart Widgets**: Line, bar, pie, scatter plots
- **Data Widgets**: Tables, metrics, KPIs
- **Input Widgets**: Model interfaces, form controls
- **Text Widgets**: Markdown, HTML content

### 2. Layout System
- Grid-based responsive layout
- Drag-and-drop widget positioning
- Configurable widget sizes
- Layout persistence

### 3. Data Binding
- Connect widgets to workflow node outputs
- Real-time data updates
- Data transformation pipelines
- Error handling and fallbacks

### 4. Configuration Management
- JSON-based dashboard configs
- Environment-based API connections
- Theme and styling options
- Import/export capabilities

## API Design

### Dashboard Endpoints
\```
GET    /api/v1/dashboards/:id
POST   /api/v1/dashboards
PUT    /api/v1/dashboards/:id
DELETE /api/v1/dashboards/:id

GET    /api/v1/dashboards/:id/widgets/:widgetId/data
POST   /api/v1/dashboards/:id/widgets
PUT    /api/v1/dashboards/:id/widgets/:widgetId
DELETE /api/v1/dashboards/:id/widgets/:widgetId
\```

### Data Access Endpoints
\```
GET /api/v1/agents/:agentId/latest-execution
GET /api/v1/nodes/:nodeId/output
GET /api/v1/executions/:executionId/results
\```

### Real-time Updates
\```
WebSocket: /ws/dashboard/:dashboardId
Server-Sent Events: /api/v1/dashboards/:id/stream
\```

## Security Considerations

1. **API Authentication**: JWT tokens for dashboard access
2. **CORS Configuration**: Proper cross-origin setup
3. **Data Sanitization**: Clean node outputs before display
4. **Rate Limiting**: Prevent API abuse
5. **Input Validation**: Validate all configuration data

## Performance Optimizations

1. **Data Caching**: Cache node outputs and execution results
2. **Lazy Loading**: Load widgets on demand
3. **Virtual Scrolling**: Handle large datasets efficiently
4. **Debounced Updates**: Batch real-time updates
5. **Compression**: Gzip API responses

## Testing Strategy

1. **Unit Tests**: Individual components and utilities
2. **Integration Tests**: Widget-to-API communication
3. **E2E Tests**: Complete dashboard workflows
4. **Performance Tests**: Load and stress testing
5. **Visual Regression**: UI consistency testing

## Deployment Options

### Development
\```bash
docker-compose up -d
# Workflow Engine: http://localhost:5000
# Dashboard: http://localhost:3001
\```

### Production
\```bash
# Option 1: Combined deployment
docker-compose -f docker-compose.prod.yml up -d

# Option 2: Separate deployment
docker build -t dashboard ./dashboard
docker run -p 3001:3000 -e VITE_WORKFLOW_API_URL=https://api.example.com dashboard
\```

## Future Enhancements

1. **Dashboard Templates**: Pre-built industry-specific dashboards
2. **Custom Widgets**: Plugin system for custom components
3. **Collaboration**: Multi-user dashboard editing
4. **Mobile App**: React Native dashboard viewer
5. **Embedding**: iframe/widget embedding for external sites
```

Tool use: **Write**

```typescript
/**
 * Dashboard System Type Definitions
 * 
 * Shared types between Workflow Engine and Dashboard Application
 */

// Core Dashboard Types
export interface Dashboard {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description?: string;
  agentId: number;
  userId: number;
  
  // Layout configuration
  layout: DashboardLayout;
  widgets: DashboardWidget[];
  
  // Display settings
  theme: DashboardTheme;
  refreshInterval?: number; // milliseconds
  
  // Metadata
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
  version: string; // for compatibility tracking
}

export interface DashboardLayout {
  grid: {
    cols: number;
    rows: number;
    gap: number;
  };
  responsive: boolean;
  compactType?: 'vertical' | 'horizontal' | null;
}

// Widget System Types
export interface DashboardWidget {
  id: string;
  type: WidgetType;
  
  // Grid position
  position: WidgetPosition;
  
  // Data source configuration
  dataSource: WidgetDataSource;
  
  // Widget-specific configuration
  config: WidgetConfig;
  
  // Display properties
  title?: string;
  description?: string;
  showHeader?: boolean;
  
  // State
  isLoading?: boolean;
  error?: string;
  lastUpdated?: Date;
}

export type WidgetType = 
  | 'chart'
  | 'table'
  | 'metric'
  | 'model-interface'
  | 'text'
  | 'image'
  | 'iframe';

export interface WidgetPosition {
  x: number;
  y: number;
  w: number; // width in grid units
  h: number; // height in grid units
  minW?: number;
  maxW?: number;
  minH?: number;
  maxH?: number;
  isDraggable?: boolean;
  isResizable?: boolean;
}

export interface WidgetDataSource {
  // Workflow connection
  agentId: number;
  nodeId: string;
  
  // Data extraction
  outputPath?: string; // JSONPath for nested data
  transform?: DataTransform;
  
  // Update behavior
  refreshOnWorkflowComplete: boolean;
  refreshInterval?: number; // override dashboard default
  cacheTime?: number; // cache duration in milliseconds
}

export interface DataTransform {
  type: 'filter' | 'map' | 'reduce' | 'sort' | 'custom';
  config: Record<string, any>;
  script?: string; // JavaScript transformation function
}

// Widget-specific configurations
export type WidgetConfig = 
  | ChartWidgetConfig
  | TableWidgetConfig
  | MetricWidgetConfig
  | ModelInterfaceWidgetConfig
  | TextWidgetConfig
  | ImageWidgetConfig
  | IframeWidgetConfig;

export interface ChartWidgetConfig {
  chartType: 'line' | 'bar' | 'pie' | 'scatter' | 'area' | 'radar';
  
  // Data mapping
  xAxis?: string;
  yAxis?: string | string[];
  colorBy?: string;
  
  // Styling
  colors?: string[];
  showLegend?: boolean;
  showGrid?: boolean;
  showTooltip?: boolean;
  
  // Axes configuration
  xAxisTitle?: string;
  yAxisTitle?: string;
  xAxisType?: 'category' | 'number' | 'time';
  yAxisType?: 'category' | 'number' | 'time';
  
  // Chart-specific options
  options?: Record<string, any>;
}

export interface TableWidgetConfig {
  // Column configuration
  columns?: TableColumn[];
  
  // Display options
  showHeader?: boolean;
  showFooter?: boolean;
  showPagination?: boolean;
  pageSize?: number;
  
  // Sorting and filtering
  sortable?: boolean;
  filterable?: boolean;
  searchable?: boolean;
  
  // Styling
  striped?: boolean;
  bordered?: boolean;
  hover?: boolean;
  
  // Export options
  exportable?: boolean;
  exportFormats?: ('csv' | 'json' | 'xlsx')[];
}

export interface TableColumn {
  key: string;
  title: string;
  width?: number;
  sortable?: boolean;
  filterable?: boolean;
  formatter?: 'number' | 'currency' | 'date' | 'percentage' | 'custom';
  formatterConfig?: Record<string, any>;
}

export interface MetricWidgetConfig {
  // Value display
  valueKey: string;
  format?: 'number' | 'currency' | 'percentage';
  precision?: number;
  prefix?: string;
  suffix?: string;
  
  // Comparison
  comparisonKey?: string;
  comparisonType?: 'absolute' | 'percentage';
  showTrend?: boolean;
  
  // Styling
  size?: 'small' | 'medium' | 'large';
  color?: string;
  icon?: string;
  
  // Thresholds
  thresholds?: MetricThreshold[];
}

export interface MetricThreshold {
  value: number;
  color: string;
  operator: 'gt' | 'gte' | 'lt' | 'lte' | 'eq';
}

export interface ModelInterfaceWidgetConfig {
  modelId: string;
  
  // Input configuration
  inputs: ModelInput[];
  
  // Output display
  outputFormat?: 'number' | 'text' | 'json' | 'chart';
  outputKey?: string;
  
  // UI options
  showInputLabels?: boolean;
  submitButtonText?: string;
  showPredictionHistory?: boolean;
}

export interface ModelInput {
  key: string;
  label: string;
  type: 'number' | 'text' | 'select' | 'checkbox';
  required?: boolean;
  defaultValue?: any;
  validation?: {
    min?: number;
    max?: number;
    pattern?: string;
    options?: string[];
  };
}

export interface TextWidgetConfig {
  content: string;
  format: 'plain' | 'markdown' | 'html';
  
  // Styling
  fontSize?: number;
  fontWeight?: 'normal' | 'bold';
  textAlign?: 'left' | 'center' | 'right';
  color?: string;
  backgroundColor?: string;
  
  // Dynamic content
  templateVariables?: Record<string, string>;
}

export interface ImageWidgetConfig {
  src: string;
  alt?: string;
  
  // Display options
  fit?: 'cover' | 'contain' | 'fill' | 'scale-down';
  showCaption?: boolean;
  caption?: string;
}

export interface IframeWidgetConfig {
  src: string;
  sandbox?: string[];
  allowFullscreen?: boolean;
}

// Theme System
export interface DashboardTheme {
  name: string;
  
  // Colors
  colors: {
    primary: string;
    secondary: string;
    background: string;
    surface: string;
    text: {
      primary: string;
      secondary: string;
      muted: string;
    };
    border: string;
    success: string;
    warning: string;
    error: string;
  };
  
  // Typography
  fonts: {
    primary: string;
    secondary?: string;
  };
  
  // Spacing
  spacing: {
    xs: number;
    sm: number;
    md: number;
    lg: number;
    xl: number;
  };
  
  // Border radius
  borderRadius: {
    sm: number;
    md: number;
    lg: number;
  };
  
  // Shadows
  shadows: {
    sm: string;
    md: string;
    lg: string;
  };
}

// API Response Types
export interface DashboardDataResponse {
  success: boolean;
  data: any;
  error?: string;
  timestamp: Date;
  executionId?: string;
}

export interface WidgetDataResponse {
  widgetId: string;
  data: any;
  error?: string;
  lastUpdated: Date;
  isStale: boolean;
}

// Real-time Update Types
export interface DashboardUpdate {
  type: 'widget-data' | 'widget-config' | 'layout' | 'error';
  dashboardId: string;
  widgetId?: string;
  data: any;
  timestamp: Date;
}

// Configuration and Settings
export interface DashboardSettings {
  apiUrl: string;
  apiKey?: string;
  
  // Performance
  maxConcurrentRequests: number;
  requestTimeout: number;
  retryAttempts: number;
  
  // Updates
  enableRealTimeUpdates: boolean;
  defaultRefreshInterval: number;
  
  // UI
  showGridLines: boolean;
  enableDragDrop: boolean;
  compactLayout: boolean;
}

// Validation and Error Types
export interface ValidationError {
  field: string;
  message: string;
  code: string;
}

export interface DashboardError {
  code: string;
  message: string;
  details?: Record<string, any>;
  timestamp: Date;
}

// Export utilities for type guards
export const isChartWidget = (widget: DashboardWidget): widget is DashboardWidget & { config: ChartWidgetConfig } => {
  return widget.type === 'chart';
};

export const isTableWidget = (widget: DashboardWidget): widget is DashboardWidget & { config: TableWidgetConfig } => {
  return widget.type === 'table';
};

export const isMetricWidget = (widget: DashboardWidget): widget is DashboardWidget & { config: MetricWidgetConfig } => {
  return widget.type === 'metric';
};

export const isModelInterfaceWidget = (widget: DashboardWidget): widget is DashboardWidget & { config: ModelInterfaceWidgetConfig } => {
  return widget.type === 'model-interface';
};
```

import { resolve } from 'path';

// https://vitejs.dev/config/
export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  
  // Path resolution
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': resolve(__dirname, 'src'),
      '@shared': resolve(__dirname, '../shared'),
    },
  },
  
  // Development server
  server: {
    port: 3001,
    host: true, // Allow external connections
    cors: true,
    proxy: {
      // Proxy API calls to workflow engine during development
      '/api': {
        target: process.env.VITE_WORKFLOW_API_URL || 'http://localhost:5000',
        changeOrigin: true,
        secure: false,
      },
    },
  },
  
  // Build configuration
  build: {
    outDir: 'dist',
    sourcemap: true,
    target: 'esnext',
    minify: 'esbuild',
    
    // Chunk splitting for better caching
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          vendor: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
          charts: ['recharts'],
          grid: ['react-grid-layout'],
          utils: ['lodash-es', 'date-fns', 'clsx'],
        },
      },
    },
    
    // Performance budgets
    chunkSizeWarningLimit: 1000,
  },
  
  // Environment variables
  define: {
    __APP_VERSION__: JSON.stringify(process.env.npm_package_version),
  },
  
  // Testing configuration
  test: {
    globals: true,
    environment: 'jsdom',
    setupFiles: ['./src/test/setup.ts'],
    coverage: {
      provider: 'v8',
      reporter: ['text', 'json', 'html'],
      exclude: [
        'node_modules/',
        'src/test/',
        '**/*.d.ts',
        '**/*.config.*',
        '**/coverage/**',
      ],
    },
  },
  
  // Optimization
  optimizeDeps: {
    include: [
      'react',
      'react-dom',
      'react-router-dom',
      'zustand',
      '@tanstack/react-query',
      'recharts',

```typescript
/**
 * Test Setup Configuration
 * 
 * Global test setup for Vitest and React Testing Library
 */

import '@testing-library/jest-dom';
import { cleanup } from '@testing-library/react';
import { afterEach, beforeAll, afterAll } from 'vitest';

// MSW for API mocking
import { setupServer } from 'msw/node';
import { handlers } from './mocks/handlers';

// Setup MSW server
export const server = setupServer(...handlers);

// Start server before all tests
beforeAll(() => {
  server.listen({ onUnhandledRequest: 'error' });
});

// Clean up after each test
afterEach(() => {
  cleanup();
  server.resetHandlers();
});

// Close server after all tests
afterAll(() => {
  server.close();
});

// Mock ResizeObserver
global.ResizeObserver = class ResizeObserver {
  observe() {}
  unobserve() {}
  disconnect() {}
};

// Mock IntersectionObserver
global.IntersectionObserver = class IntersectionObserver {
  constructor() {}
  observe() {}
  unobserve() {}
  disconnect() {}
};

// Mock matchMedia
Object.defineProperty(window, 'matchMedia', {
  writable: true,
  value: (query: string) => ({
    matches: false,
    media: query,
    onchange: null,
    addListener: () => {},
    removeListener: () => {},
    addEventListener: () => {},
    removeEventListener: () => {},
    dispatchEvent: () => {},
  }),
});

// Mock scrollTo
Object.defineProperty(window, 'scrollTo', {
  writable: true,
  value: () => {},
});

// Environment variables for testing
process.env.VITE_WORKFLOW_API_URL = 'http://localhost:5000';
process.env.VITE_APP_VERSION = '1.0.0-test';
```

    },
    fonts: {
      primary: 'Inter, system-ui, sans-serif',
    },
    spacing: { xs: 4, sm: 8, md: 16, lg: 24, xl: 32 },
    borderRadius: { sm: 4, md: 8, lg: 12 },
    shadows: {
      sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
      md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)',
      lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)',
    },
  },
  refreshInterval: 30000,
  createdAt: new Date('2024-01-01'),
  updatedAt: new Date('2024-01-01'),
  version: '1.0.0',
};

const mockWidgetData = {
  'widget-1': [
    { date: '2024-01-01', value: 100 },
    { date: '2024-01-02', value: 150 },
    { date: '2024-01-03', value: 200 },
  ],
  'widget-2': { total: 450, change: '+12%' },
};

export const handlers = [
  // Dashboard CRUD
  http.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/dashboards/:id`, ({ params }) => {
    const { id } = params;
    if (id === 'dashboard-1') {
      return HttpResponse.json({
        success: true,
        data: mockDashboard,
        timestamp: new Date(),
      } as ApiResponse<Dashboard>);
    }
    return HttpResponse.json(
      {
        success: false,
        error: 'Dashboard not found',
        timestamp: new Date(),
      },
      { status: 404 }
    );
  }),

  http.post(`${API_BASE_URL}/dashboards`, async ({ request }) => {
    const data = await request.json();
    return HttpResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: { ...mockDashboard, ...data, id: 'new-dashboard' },
      timestamp: new Date(),
    } as ApiResponse<Dashboard>);
  }),

  http.put(`${API_BASE_URL}/dashboards/:id`, async ({ params, request }) => {
    const { id } = params;
    const data = await request.json();
    return HttpResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: { ...mockDashboard, ...data, id },
      timestamp: new Date(),
    } as ApiResponse<Dashboard>);
  }),

  http.delete(`${API_BASE_URL}/dashboards/:id`, ({ params }) => {
    return HttpResponse.json({
      success: true,
      timestamp: new Date(),
    } as ApiResponse);
  }),

  // Widget data
  http.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/dashboards/:dashboardId/widgets/:widgetId/data`, ({ params }) => {
    const { widgetId } = params;
    const data = mockWidgetData[widgetId as keyof typeof mockWidgetData];
    
    if (data) {
      return HttpResponse.json({
        success: true,
        data,
        timestamp: new Date(),
      } as ApiResponse);
    }
    
    return HttpResponse.json(
      {
        success: false,
        error: 'Widget data not found',
        timestamp: new Date(),
      },
      { status: 404 }
    );
  }),

  // Node outputs
  http.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/nodes/:nodeId/output`, ({ params }) => {
    const { nodeId } = params;
    
    const outputs = {
      'node-1': mockWidgetData['widget-1'],
      'node-2': mockWidgetData['widget-2'],
    };
    
    const data = outputs[nodeId as keyof typeof outputs];
    
    if (data) {
      return HttpResponse.json({
        success: true,
        data,
        timestamp: new Date(),
      } as ApiResponse);
    }
    
    return HttpResponse.json(
      {
        success: false,
        error: 'Node output not found',
        timestamp: new Date(),
      },
      { status: 404 }
    );
  }),

  // Agent executions
  http.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/agents/:agentId/latest-execution`, ({ params }) => {
    return HttpResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        id: 'execution-1',
        agentId: params.agentId,
        status: 'completed',
        startedAt: new Date('2024-01-01T10:00:00Z'),
        completedAt: new Date('2024-01-01T10:05:00Z'),
        results: mockWidgetData,
      },
      timestamp: new Date(),
    } as ApiResponse);
  }),

  // Error simulation for testing
  http.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/error`, () => {
    return HttpResponse.json(
      {
        success: false,
        error: 'Internal server error',
        timestamp: new Date(),
      },
      { status: 500 }
    );
  }),
];
```

/**
 * Test Utilities
 * 
 * Custom render functions and test helpers
 */

import React, { ReactElement } from 'react';
import { render, RenderOptions } from '@testing-library/react';
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { BrowserRouter } from 'react-router-dom';
import { vi } from 'vitest';

// Test providers wrapper
interface AllTheProvidersProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

const AllTheProviders = ({ children }: AllTheProvidersProps) => {
  // Create a new QueryClient for each test to avoid cache pollution
  const queryClient = new QueryClient({
    defaultOptions: {
      queries: {
        retry: false,
        gcTime: 0,
      },
      mutations: {
        retry: false,
      },
    },
  });

  return (
    <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
      <BrowserRouter>
        <div id="portal-root" />
        {children}
      </BrowserRouter>
    </QueryClientProvider>
  );
};

const customRender = (
  ui: ReactElement,
  options?: Omit<RenderOptions, 'wrapper'>
) => render(ui, { wrapper: AllTheProviders, ...options });

export * from '@testing-library/react';
export { customRender as render };

// Common test helpers
export const createMockWidget = (overrides = {}) => ({
  id: 'test-widget',
  type: 'chart' as const,
  position: { x: 0, y: 0, w: 6, h: 4 },
  dataSource: {
    agentId: 1,
    nodeId: 'test-node',
    refreshOnWorkflowComplete: true,
  },
  config: {
    chartType: 'line' as const,
    xAxis: 'date',
    yAxis: 'value',
  },
  title: 'Test Widget',
  ...overrides,
});

export const createMockDashboard = (overrides = {}) => ({
  id: 'test-dashboard',
  name: 'Test Dashboard',
  agentId: 1,
  userId: 1,
  layout: {
    grid: { cols: 12, rows: 8, gap: 16 },
    responsive: true,
  },
  widgets: [createMockWidget()],
  theme: {
    name: 'default',
    colors: {
      primary: '#3b82f6',
      secondary: '#64748b',
      background: '#ffffff',
      surface: '#f8fafc',
      text: {
        primary: '#1e293b',
        secondary: '#475569',
        muted: '#94a3b8',
      },
      border: '#e2e8f0',
      success: '#22c55e',
      warning: '#f59e0b',
      error: '#ef4444',
    },
    fonts: { primary: 'Inter' },
    spacing: { xs: 4, sm: 8, md: 16, lg: 24, xl: 32 },
    borderRadius: { sm: 4, md: 8, lg: 12 },
    shadows: {
      sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
      md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)',
      lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)',
    },
  },
  createdAt: new Date(),
  updatedAt: new Date(),
  version: '1.0.0',
  ...overrides,
});

// Mock functions
export const mockApiCall = vi.fn();
export const mockWebSocket = {
  send: vi.fn(),
  close: vi.fn(),
  addEventListener: vi.fn(),
  removeEventListener: vi.fn(),
};

// Wait for async operations
export const waitForAsyncOperations = () =>
  new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 0));

// Resize observer mock for grid layout tests
export const mockResizeObserver = () => {
  const mockObserver = vi.fn(() => ({
    observe: vi.fn(),
    unobserve: vi.fn(),
    disconnect: vi.fn(),
  }));
  
  vi.stubGlobal('ResizeObserver', mockObserver);
  
  return mockObserver;
};

// Local storage mock
export const mockLocalStorage = () => {
  const store: Record<string, string> = {};
  
  return {
    getItem: vi.fn((key: string) => store[key] || null),
    setItem: vi.fn((key: string, value: string) => {
      store[key] = value;
    }),
    removeItem: vi.fn((key: string) => {
      delete store[key];
    }),
    clear: vi.fn(() => {
      Object.keys(store).forEach(key => delete store[key]);
    }),
    length: Object.keys(store).length,
    key: vi.fn((index: number) => Object.keys(store)[index] || null),
  };
};

 * @see https://playwright.dev/docs/test-configuration.

export default defineConfig({
  testDir: './src/test/e2e',
  /* Run tests in files in parallel */
  fullyParallel: true,
  /* Fail the build on CI if you accidentally left test.only in the source code. */
  forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI,
  /* Retry on CI only */
  retries: process.env.CI ? 2 : 0,
  /* Opt out of parallel tests on CI. */
  workers: process.env.CI ? 1 : undefined,
  /* Reporter to use. See https://playwright.dev/docs/test-reporters */
  reporter: [
    ['html'],
    ['json', { outputFile: 'test-results/results.json' }],
    ['junit', { outputFile: 'test-results/results.xml' }],
  ],
  /* Shared settings for all the projects below. See https://playwright.dev/docs/api/class-testoptions. */
  use: {
    /* Base URL to use in actions like `await page.goto('/')`. */
    baseURL: 'http://localhost:3001',

    /* Collect trace when retrying the failed test. See https://playwright.dev/docs/trace-viewer */
    trace: 'on-first-retry',

<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <link rel="icon" type="image/svg+xml" href="/dashboard-icon.svg" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Workflow Dashboard</title>
    <meta name="description" content="Professional dashboard for Workflow Engine data visualization" />
    
    <!-- Preload critical fonts -->
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@300;400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    
    <!-- Prevent FOUC -->
    <style>
      html { visibility: hidden; }
      html.fonts-loaded { visibility: visible; }
    </style>
    
    <!-- Font loading optimization -->
    <script>
      (function() {
        if (sessionStorage.getItem('fonts-loaded')) {
          document.documentElement.classList.add('fonts-loaded');
        } else {
          document.fonts.ready.then(function() {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('fonts-loaded');
            sessionStorage.setItem('fonts-loaded', 'true');
          });
        }
      })();
    </script>
  </head>
  <body>
    <div id="root"></div>
    <div id="portal-root"></div>
    <script type="module" src="/src/main.tsx"></script>
  </body>
</html>
```

    @apply border-border;

    @apply bg-background text-foreground font-sans antialiased;

    font-variation-settings: 'opsz' 32;
  }

    @apply w-2 h-2;
  }

    @apply bg-surface-100;

    @apply bg-surface-400;

  }

    @apply font-medium text-success-900;
  }

    @apply text-sm text-success-700 mt-1;
  }
}

/* Utility classes */
@layer utilities {
  /* Text utilities */
  .text-gradient {
    @apply bg-gradient-to-r from-primary-600 to-primary-800 bg-clip-text text-transparent;
  }
  
  /* Layout utilities */
  .safe-area-inset {
    padding-left: env(safe-area-inset-left);
    padding-right: env(safe-area-inset-right);
  }
  
  /* Animation utilities */
  .animate-slide-up {
    animation: slideUp 0.2s ease-out;
  }
  
  .animate-slide-down {
    animation: slideDown 0.2s ease-out;
  }
  
  .animate-fade-in {
    animation: fadeIn 0.3s ease-out;
  }
  
  /* Chart utilities */
  .chart-container {
    @apply relative w-full h-full overflow-hidden;
  }
  
  .chart-tooltip {
    @apply bg-white border border-surface-200 rounded-lg shadow-lg p-3 text-sm;
  }
  
  /* Grid utilities */
  .grid-cols-dashboard {
    grid-template-columns: repeat(12, minmax(0, 1fr));
  }
}

/* Dark mode support */
@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {
  :root.dark {
    --color-background: 15 23 42; /* slate-900 */
    --color-foreground: 248 250 252; /* slate-50 */
    --color-surface-50: 15 23 42;
    --color-surface-100: 30 41 59;
    --color-surface-200: 51 65 85;
    --color-surface-300: 71 85 105;
  }
  
  .dark .widget-container {
    @apply bg-surface-800 border-surface-700;
  }
  
  .dark .widget-header {
    @apply border-surface-700;
  }
  
  .dark .widget-title {
    @apply text-surface-100;
  }
}

/* Print styles */
@media print {
  .no-print {
    display: none !important;
  }
  
  .widget-container {
    @apply shadow-none border border-surface-300;
    break-inside: avoid;
  }
  
  .chart-container {
    @apply border border-surface-300;
  }
}

/* High contrast mode */
@media (prefers-contrast: high) {
  .widget-container {
    @apply border-2 border-surface-900;
  }
  
  .btn-primary {
    @apply border border-primary-900;
  }
}

/* Reduced motion */
@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
  * {
    animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;
    animation-iteration-count: 1 !important;
    transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;
  }
  
  .loading-spinner {
    @apply animate-none;
  }
}

Tool use: **Write**

```tsx
/**
 * Dashboard Application Entry Point
 * 
 * Main React application bootstrap with providers and error boundaries
 */

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom/client';
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { ReactQueryDevtools } from '@tanstack/react-query-devtools';
import { ErrorBoundary } from 'react-error-boundary';
import { BrowserRouter } from 'react-router-dom';

import App from './App';
import ErrorFallback from './components/ErrorFallback';
import { DashboardProvider } from './providers/DashboardProvider';
import { ThemeProvider } from './providers/ThemeProvider';

import './index.css';

// Configure React Query client
const queryClient = new QueryClient({
  defaultOptions: {
    queries: {
      staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes
      gcTime: 10 * 60 * 1000, // 10 minutes
      retry: (failureCount, error: any) => {
        // Don't retry on 4xx errors
        if (error?.status >= 400 && error?.status < 500) {
          return false;
        }
        return failureCount < 3;
      },
      refetchOnWindowFocus: false,
      refetchOnMount: true,
    },
    mutations: {
      retry: 1,
    },
  },
});

// Global error handler
const handleError = (error: Error, errorInfo: { componentStack: string }) => {
  console.error('Dashboard Application Error:', error, errorInfo);
  
  // Report to error tracking service in production
  if (import.meta.env.PROD) {
    // TODO: Integrate with error tracking service (Sentry, etc.)
  }
};

// Application root component with all providers
const AppRoot = () => (
  <ErrorBoundary
    FallbackComponent={ErrorFallback}
    onError={handleError}
    onReset={() => window.location.reload()}
  >
    <BrowserRouter>
      <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
        <ThemeProvider>
          <DashboardProvider>
            <App />
            {import.meta.env.DEV && <ReactQueryDevtools initialIsOpen={false} />}
          </DashboardProvider>
        </ThemeProvider>
      </QueryClientProvider>
    </BrowserRouter>
  </ErrorBoundary>
);

// Enable React DevTools in development
if (import.meta.env.DEV) {
  import('@tanstack/react-query-devtools').then(({ ReactQueryDevtools }) => {
    // DevTools loaded
  });
}

// Mount application
const root = ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById('root')!);

// Enable React 18 concurrent features
root.render(
  <React.StrictMode>
    <AppRoot />
  </React.StrictMode>
);

// Performance monitoring
if (import.meta.env.PROD) {
  // Web Vitals reporting
  import('web-vitals').then(({ getCLS, getFID, getFCP, getLCP, getTTFB }) => {
    const reportWebVitals = (metric: any) => {
      console.log('Web Vital:', metric);
      // TODO: Send to analytics service
    };

    getCLS(reportWebVitals);
    getFID(reportWebVitals);
    getFCP(reportWebVitals);
    getLCP(reportWebVitals);
    getTTFB(reportWebVitals);
  }).catch(() => {
    // Web vitals not available
  });
}

// Service Worker registration for PWA features (optional)
if ('serviceWorker' in navigator && import.meta.env.PROD) {
  window.addEventListener('load', () => {
    navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js')
      .then((registration) => {
        console.log('SW registered: ', registration);
      })
      .catch((registrationError) => {
        console.log('SW registration failed: ', registrationError);
      });
  });
}
```

Result:

```
File created successfully at: /Users/markmiller/workflow-engine/dashboard/src/main.tsx
```

Tool use: **Write**

```tsx
/**
 * Error Fallback Component
 * 
 * Displayed when the application encounters an unhandled error
 */

import React from 'react';
import { AlertTriangle, RefreshCw, Home } from 'lucide-react';
import { FallbackProps } from 'react-error-boundary';

interface ErrorFallbackProps extends FallbackProps {
  error: Error;
  resetErrorBoundary: () => void;
}

const ErrorFallback: React.FC<ErrorFallbackProps> = ({
  error,
  resetErrorBoundary,
}) => {
  const isDevelopment = import.meta.env.DEV;

  const handleGoHome = () => {
    window.location.href = '/';
  };

  const handleReload = () => {
    window.location.reload();
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-surface-50 px-4">
      <div className="max-w-md w-full">
        <div className="text-center">
          <div className="mx-auto h-12 w-12 text-danger-500 mb-4">
            <AlertTriangle className="h-full w-full" />
          </div>
          
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-surface-900 mb-2">
            Something went wrong
          </h1>
          
          <p className="text-surface-600 mb-6">
            We encountered an unexpected error. Please try refreshing the page or 
            return to the dashboard.
          </p>
          
          <div className="space-y-3 mb-6">
            <button
              onClick={resetErrorBoundary}
              className="w-full btn btn-primary btn-md"
            >
              <RefreshCw className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
              Try Again
            </button>
            
            <button
              onClick={handleGoHome}
              className="w-full btn btn-secondary btn-md"
            >
              <Home className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
              Go to Dashboard
            </button>
            
            <button
              onClick={handleReload}
              className="w-full btn btn-ghost btn-md"
            >
              Reload Page
            </button>
          </div>
          
          {isDevelopment && (
            <details className="text-left bg-surface-100 rounded-lg p-4">
              <summary className="cursor-pointer font-medium text-surface-700 mb-2">
                Error Details (Development)
              </summary>
              <div className="text-sm text-surface-600 space-y-2">
                <div>
                  <strong>Error:</strong> {error.name}
                </div>
                <div>
                  <strong>Message:</strong> {error.message}
                </div>
                {error.stack && (
                  <div>
                    <strong>Stack Trace:</strong>
                    <pre className="text-xs bg-surface-200 p-2 rounded mt-1 overflow-auto">
                      {error.stack}
                    </pre>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </details>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default ErrorFallback;
```
